  forwarding(From webserver to external network) + DHCP(internal network) +

<h1><a name="_Toc69809591"><span lang=EN-US>Network design of the project:</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:26.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shapetype
 id="_x0000_t75" coordsize="21600,21600" o:spt="75" o:preferrelative="t"
 path="m@4@5l@4@11@9@11@9@5xe" filled="f" stroked="f">
 <v:stroke joinstyle="miter"/>
 <v:formulas>
  <v:f eqn="if lineDrawn pixelLineWidth 0"/>

  <v:f eqn="prod @3 21600 pixelWidth"/>
  <v:f eqn="prod @3 21600 pixelHeight"/>

</v:shapetype><v:shape id="圖片_x0020_140" o:spid="_x0000_i1067" type="#_x0000_t75"

 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image005.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img width=553 height=254
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image006.png" v:shapes="圖片_x0020_140"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>In the internal network the web server will
have a web page in port 80 , that firewall need to port forwarding it to the
external network with the firewall IP. So, for the external network the website
will become IP 192.168.1.101 and port 80. Also, I have made a DNS for the
website in </span><span lang=EN-US><a
href="http://eie3117projectbitcoinexchangenet.ga/"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'>http://eie3117projectbitcoinexchangenet.ga/</span></a></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'> . That mean the kali Linux or
devices in the external network can use </span><span lang=EN-US><a
href="http://eie3117projectbitcoinexchangenet.ga/"><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'>http://eie3117projectbitcoinexchangenet.ga/</span></a></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'> or 192.168.1.101 to access the
website<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>That is the firewall setting of port forward<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_141" o:spid="_x0000_i1066" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="一張含有 文字, 螢幕擷取畫面, 監視器, 室內 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"

</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=554 height=191

lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:新細明體;mso-fareast-theme-font:

</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>Also, the only port 80 or 443 go form
external network to the internal network<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_142" o:spid="_x0000_i1065" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"

src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image010.png" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
v:shapes="圖片_x0020_142"><![endif]></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>And all the port can go from internal network
to external network <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape

v:shapes="圖片_x0020_143"><![endif]></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>This is the firewall rule<o:p></o:p></span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span class=SpellE><b><span

style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'>So, in kali Linux use Nmap to scan the
192.168.1.101 will only have port 80 and 443<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;
mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:新細明體;mso-fareast-theme-font:
minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
ZH-TW;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;
page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc69809593"><span lang=EN-US>Web GUI design:</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:
Arial'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Responsive web design (RWD) -&gt; Design cover phone,
table, and desktop<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:
Arial'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Web GUI have three parts, the information part
box will in the center<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-pagination:widow-orphan;mso-list:l6 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-fareast-font-family:
Arial'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:11.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>That makes the UI can fit both the mobile and
desktop.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>This is the design pattern
of the web UI.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:26.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_144" o:spid="_x0000_i1063" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:278.25pt;
 height:210pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image013.png" o:title=""
  cropleft="358f"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=371 height=280
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image014.png" v:shapes="圖片_x0020_144"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:26.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2><a name="_Toc69809594"><span lang=EN-US>Web GUI design: (QR code)</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>The receive
address will use JavaScript to Generate QR code(For phone wallet users) The QR code
is (“Bitcoin:&lt;receive address&gt;”)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:26.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_147" o:spid="_x0000_i1060" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:173.25pt;

<h2><a name="_Toc69809595"><span lang=EN-US>Web GUI design: (Check Password)</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Check password
is correct or not can clearly show the password requirement<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:
yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="圖片_x0020_148" o:spid="_x0000_i1059"

<h2><a name="_Toc69809596"><span lang=EN-US>Web GUI design: (Loading animation)</span></a></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>In some pages
need to wait few seconds(such as Record and Personal information) add some
loading animation, that let the user know is loading the page. It is not no
responsive and make the page eyes catching.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape id="圖片_x0020_159" o:spid="_x0000_i1058"

<h3><a name="_Toc69809598"><span lang=EN-US>Process in Signa up an account</span></a></h3>

  <p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:

  </span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Go
  to the sign-up page (From index page signup button or login page ”Want<span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp; </span>a new account”)<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:rect

<h1><a name="_Toc69809603"><span lang=EN-US>Database design</span></a></h1>

<h4><span lang=EN-US>Database: <span class=SpellE>Bitcoin_Exchange_website</span></span></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_166" o:spid="_x0000_i1029" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:414.75pt;
 height:213pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image105.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=553 height=284
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image105.png" v:shapes="圖片_x0020_166"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>The database will have one account:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l5 level1 lfo7'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:Arial'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>management
account (only can insert data and update data)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>All the function of the website only needs
insert and update to achieve it.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:新細明體;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all
style='mso-special-character:line-break;page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc69809604"><span lang=EN-US>Security evaluation:</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc69809604'></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:300%'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Apache:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>mod_security</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>This <span class=SpellE>apache</span> module
can detect the attack and defense it (Such as SQL injection Attacks,</span><span
lang=EN-US> </span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Cross-site Scripting or</span><span lang=EN-US>
</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Path
Traversal Attacks). In server use OWASP <span class=SpellE>ModSecurity</span> core
rule Set to become the rule.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_170" o:spid="_x0000_i1028" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:152.25pt;
 height:129.75pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image106.png" o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=203 height=173
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image107.png" v:shapes="圖片_x0020_170"><![endif]></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>&nbsp;</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_171" o:spid="_x0000_i1027" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
 style='width:234pt;height:77.25pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image108.png" o:title="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=312 height=103
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image109.png" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
v:shapes="圖片_x0020_171"><![endif]></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>mod_evasive</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>The <span class=SpellE>apache</span> module can
protect the web server that is having dos attack.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>PHP:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Google reCAPTCHA<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>User to identify the user is robot or not.</span><span
lang=EN-US> </span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Avoid malicious registration of robots or
interested persons to affect the website.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_168" o:spid="_x0000_i1026" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
 style='width:186pt;height:51.75pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image110.png" o:title="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=248 height=69
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image111.png" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
v:shapes="圖片_x0020_168"><![endif]></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Firewall:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Only allow the port with is in needed. So, the
firewall only open port 80,443.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif;mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="圖片_x0020_169" o:spid="_x0000_i1025" type="#_x0000_t75" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
 style='width:415.5pt;height:89.25pt;visibility:visible;mso-wrap-style:square'>
 <v:imagedata src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image112.png" o:title="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
  croptop="15713f" cropbottom="8640f"/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=554 height=119
src="EIE3117%20Final%20report.files/image113.png" alt="一張含有 文字 的圖片&#10;&#10;自動產生的描述"
v:shapes="圖片_x0020_169"><![endif]></span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Website:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:"Arial",sans-serif'>Will check the user input only allow specific
character such as(input price only can input float number). So, input have
specific value will use hash to check it such as (Login ID or password)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1><a name="_Toc69809605"><span lang=EN-US>Difficulties</span></a></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The bitcoin wallet is difficult to set up,
for example, I need to know how many coins used to deposit and withdraw. I make
a specific address for the user and let them deposit their coin, finally, it
can check how many users save coins in the address. Generate a specific address
only allow withdrawals to specific users</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The firewall port forwarding is difficult
to do it. It is because the set up always not working or apply. I set up and
reset 5 time and it work.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Firewall and the web server network are not
stable. Sometimes the firewall and the web server will suddenly disconnect to
the internet. To make it stable , I only set it with static IP and always save
the status of web server and firewall in snapshot. That make it more stable and
restore it when the network has problem.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The crypto wallet is difficult to set up,
so I ask my friend and watch how to set up it, finally the setup is done.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>It difficult to save the image into
database, so I change the way save the image into specific location and give
them a unit id for the file. The database only saves the image name.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;font-family:
"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:
新細明體;mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";mso-bidi-theme-font:minor-bidi;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:ZH-TW;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br
clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan'><b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:26.0pt;font-family:"Calibri Light",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
major-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:新細明體;mso-fareast-theme-font:major-fareast;

mso-bidi-theme-font:major-bidi;mso-font-kerning:26.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
